We have a constrained housing supply ‚Äì simply not enough homes being built or coming onto the market. On top of that, we have strong, sustained buyer demand. This potent combination has already driven home prices sky-high over the past few years. Now, add in higher mortgage interest rates, which drastically increase the monthly cost of borrowing for those already expensive homes.\n\nThe result?
